    26â†’// Function to inject content into HTML file
    27â†’function injectContentIntoHtml(filePath) {
    28â†’    try {
    29â†’        let htmlContent = fs.readFileSync(filePath, 'utf8');
    30â†’

    32â†’        if (htmlContent.includes('ENCRYPTED_CORPORATE_CONTENT_START')) {
    33â†’            console.log('â­ï¸  Already injected:', path.relative(SITE_DIR, filePath));
    34â†’            return;
    35â†’        }
    36â†’

    40â†’${encryptedContent}
    41â†’ENCRYPTED_CORPORATE_CONTENT_END -->`;
    42â†’

    44â†’        if (htmlContent.includes('</body>')) {

    48â†’        } else {
    49â†’            console.log('âš ï¸  No </body> tag found in:', path.relative(SITE_DIR, filePath));
    50â†’        }
    51â†’    } catch (error) {

    53â†’    }

    55â†’
    56â†’// Recursively find and process HTML files
    57â†’function processDirectory(dirPath) {
    58â†’    const entries = fs.readdirSync(dirPath, { withFileTypes: true });
    59â†’    
    60â†’    for (const entry of entries) {

    62â†’

   275â†’        const corporateElements = document.querySelectorAll('.bmw-corporate-only');
   276â†’        console.log(`Found ${corporateElements.length} corporate elements to hide`);
   277â†’        corporateElements.forEach(element => {
   278â†’            element.classList.remove('show-corporate');
   279â†’            element.classList.remove('corporate-network-detected');
   280â†’        });
   281â†’
   282â†’        const publicElements = document.querySelectorAll('.bmw-public-alternative');
   283â†’        console.log(`Found ${publicElements.length} public elements to show`);
   284â†’        publicElements.forEach(element => {
   285â†’            element.classList.remove('hide-public');
   286â†’            element.classList.add('public-network-detected');
   287â†’        });
   288â†’
   289â†’        // Hide corporate navigation items and show public ones  
   290â†’        hideCorporateNavigationItems();
   291â†’        showPublicNavigationItems();
   292â†’        removeSession10Navigation();
   293â†’
   294â†’        console.log('ğŸ“‹ Public mode: public content visible');
   295â†’        
   296â†’
   297â†’        // Update any dynamic text content
   298â†’        updateNetworkSpecificContent(false);
   299â†’        
   300â†’        // Update network status indicator
   301â†’        updateNetworkStatusIndicator('public');
   302â†’    }

   334â†’    function updateNetworkStatusIndicator(networkType) {

   336â†’        const currentPath = window.location.pathname;
   337â†’        const isSetupPage = currentPath.includes('00_intro') || 
   338â†’                           currentPath.includes('setup') ||

   341â†’                           currentPath.includes('llmapi');

   383â†’                    Checking corporate access
   384â†’                </div>

   400â†’            'BMW Corporate Network - Cloud Development Environment Available' :

   411â†’                    if (indicator && indicator.parentNode) {
   412â†’                        indicator.remove();

   419â†’    function initializeNetworkDetection() {
   420â†’        // Add CSS for smooth transitions and ensure BMW content is hidden by default on public sites
   421â†’        const style = document.createElement('style');
   422â†’        const hostname = window.location.hostname;
   423â†’        const isPublicSite = hostname.includes('github.io') || hostname.includes('fwornle');
   424â†’        
   425â†’        style.textContent = `
   426â†’            /* Default: hide all conditional content until detection completes */
   427â†’            .bmw-corporate-only {
   428â†’                display: none;
   429â†’                transition: opacity 0.3s ease-in-out;
   430â†’            }
   431â†’            .bmw-public-alternative {
   432â†’                display: none;
   433â†’                transition: opacity 0.3s ease-in-out;
   434â†’            }
   435â†’            /* Show corporate content when detected */
   436â†’            .bmw-corporate-only.corporate-network-detected {
   437â†’                display: block;
   438â†’                animation: fadeIn 0.5s ease-in-out;
   439â†’            }
   440â†’            /* Show public content when detected */
   441â†’            .bmw-public-alternative.public-network-detected {
   442â†’                display: block;
   443â†’                animation: fadeIn 0.5s ease-in-out;
   444â†’            }
   445â†’            @keyframes fadeIn {
   446â†’                from { opacity: 0; }
   447â†’                to { opacity: 1; }
   448â†’            }
   449â†’            /* Ensure setup instructions container is visible */
   450â†’            .setup-instructions {
   451â†’                min-height: 100px;
   452â†’            }
   453â†’        `;
   454â†’        document.head.appendChild(style);
   455â†’
   456â†’        // Always run CN detection regardless of hostname
   457â†’        console.log('Running corporate network detection...');
   458â†’        
   459â†’        // Initial quick check, then run full detection
   460â†’        if (isCorporateNetwork()) {
   461â†’            console.log('Corporate network detected initially');
   462â†’            showCorporateContent();
   463â†’        } else {
   464â†’            console.log('Public network assumed initially, running full CN detection');
   465â†’            hideCorporateContent();
   466â†’            // Always run the comprehensive check for CN access
   467â†’            checkInternalService();
   468â†’        }
   469â†’    }
   470â†’
   471â†’    function cleanupNavigationState() {
   472â†’        // Clean up any previous navigation state
   473â†’        // We're on a corporate page, so just reset for fresh setup
   474â†’        if (window.corporateScrollListener) {
   475â†’            window.removeEventListener('scroll', window.corporateScrollListener);
   476â†’            window.corporateScrollListener = null;
   477â†’            console.log('ğŸ§¹ Cleaned up previous corporate scroll listener');
   478â†’        }
   479â†’    }
   480â†’
   481â†’    // Initialize when DOM is ready and on every page load
   482â†’    function runDetection() {
   483â†’        // Prevent multiple simultaneous detections
   484â†’        if (detectionInProgress) {
   485â†’            console.log('ğŸ”„ Detection already in progress, skipping...');
   486â†’            return;
   487â†’        }
   488â†’        
   489â†’        // Clear any pending detection
   490â†’        if (detectionTimeout) {
   491â†’            clearTimeout(detectionTimeout);
   492â†’        }
   493â†’        
   494â†’        // Aggressive debounce to prevent rapid successive calls from different event sources
   495â†’        detectionTimeout = setTimeout(() => {
   496â†’            // Double-check as detection might have been triggered by another source
   497â†’            if (detectionInProgress) {
   498â†’                console.log('ğŸ”„ Detection started by another trigger, skipping...');
   499â†’                return;
   500â†’            }
   501â†’            
   502â†’            detectionInProgress = true;
   503â†’            console.log('ğŸ”„ Starting fresh network detection...');
   504â†’            
   505â†’            // Clean up navigation state first
   506â†’            cleanupNavigationState();
   507â†’            
   508â†’            try {
   509â†’                initializeNetworkDetection();
   510â†’            } finally {
   511â†’                // Reset detection flag after longer delay to prevent rapid re-runs
   512â†’                setTimeout(() => {
   513â†’                    detectionInProgress = false;
   514â†’                    console.log('âœ… Network detection cycle complete, ready for next run');
   515â†’                }, 5000); // Increased from 2000 to 5000ms
   516â†’            }
   517â†’        }, 300); // Increased from 100 to 300ms debounce delay
   518â†’    }
   519â†’    
   520â†’    // Initial run
   521â†’    if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
   522â†’        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', runDetection);
   523â†’    } else {
   524â†’        runDetection();
   525â†’    }
   526â†’    
   527â†’    // Set up navigation listeners immediately (not waiting for DOMContentLoaded)
   528â†’    console.log('ğŸ¯ Setting up navigation listeners');
   529â†’    
   530â†’    // Watch for URL changes with MutationObserver
   531â†’    let lastUrl = location.href;
   532â†’    const observer = new MutationObserver(() => {
   533â†’        const url = location.href;
   534â†’        if (url !== lastUrl) {
   535â†’            lastUrl = url;
   536â†’            console.log('ğŸ“ URL changed to:', url);
   537â†’            
   538â†’            // Reset Session 10 loaded flag when navigating to different pages
   539â†’            if (!url.includes('session10-corporate') && !url.includes('Session10_Enterprise_Integration')) {
   540â†’                session10Loaded = false;
   541â†’            }
   542â†’            
   543â†’            // No cleanup needed - if we navigate away, the page will reload
   544â†’            // and our early exit will prevent this code from running
   545â†’            
   546â†’            setTimeout(runDetection, 100);
   547â†’        }
   548â†’    });
   549â†’    observer.observe(document.body || document.documentElement, {
   550â†’        subtree: true, 
   551â†’        childList: true
   552â†’    });
   553â†’    
   554â†’    // Listen for navigation link clicks (use capturing to catch all clicks)
   555â†’    document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
   556â†’        const link = e.target.closest('a');
   557â†’        if (link) {
   558â†’            const href = link.getAttribute('href');
   559â†’            console.log('ğŸ”— Link clicked:', href);
   560â†’            if (link.classList.contains('md-nav__link') || 
   561â†’                link.classList.contains('md-tabs__link') ||
   562â†’                href?.includes('/00_intro/')) {
   563â†’                console.log('ğŸ”— Navigation link detected, will re-run detection');
   564â†’                setTimeout(runDetection, 500);
   565â†’            }
   566â†’        }
   567â†’    }, true); // Use capture phase
   568â†’    
   569â†’    // Also listen for popstate
   570â†’    window.addEventListener('popstate', () => {
   571â†’        console.log('â¬…ï¸ Browser navigation detected');
   572â†’        
   573â†’        // Reset Session 10 loaded flag when navigating back/forward
   574â†’        const url = location.href;
   575â†’        if (!url.includes('session10-corporate') && !url.includes('Session10_Enterprise_Integration')) {
   576â†’            session10Loaded = false;
   577â†’        }
   578â†’        
   579â†’        runDetection();
   580â†’    });
   581â†’
   582â†’    // Navigation control functions
   583â†’    function hideCorporateNavigationItems() {
   584â†’        const navigationItems = document.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__link');
   585â†’        navigationItems.forEach(link => {
   586â†’            const linkText = link.textContent.trim();
   587â†’            // Hide items that contain corporate/BMW content indicators
   588â†’            if (linkText.includes('BMW Gaia LLM API') || 
   589â†’                linkText.includes('BMW Cloud Development Environment with Coder') ||
   590â†’                linkText.includes('Quick Setup') ||
   591â†’                linkText.includes('Testing Your Connection') ||
   592â†’                linkText.includes('Available Models') ||
   593â†’                linkText.includes('Using in Code') ||
   594â†’                linkText.includes('Framework Integration') ||
   595â†’                linkText.includes('Why Cloud Development?') ||
   596â†’                linkText.includes('AI Assistant Integration')) {
   597â†’                const listItem = link.closest('.md-nav__item');
   598â†’                if (listItem) {
   599â†’                    console.log('Hiding corporate nav item:', linkText);
   600â†’                    listItem.style.display = 'none';
   601â†’                }
   602â†’            }
   603â†’        });
   604â†’    }
   605â†’
   606â†’    function showCorporateNavigationItems() {
   607â†’        const navigationItems = document.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__link');
   608â†’        navigationItems.forEach(link => {
   609â†’            const linkText = link.textContent.trim();
   610â†’            // Show items that contain corporate/BMW content indicators
   611â†’            if (linkText.includes('BMW Gaia LLM API') || 
   612â†’                linkText.includes('BMW Cloud Development Environment with Coder') ||
   613â†’                linkText.includes('Quick Setup') ||
   614â†’                linkText.includes('Testing Your Connection') ||
   615â†’                linkText.includes('Available Models') ||
   616â†’                linkText.includes('Using in Code') ||
   617â†’                linkText.includes('Framework Integration') ||
   618â†’                linkText.includes('Why Cloud Development?') ||
   619â†’                linkText.includes('AI Assistant Integration')) {
   620â†’                const listItem = link.closest('.md-nav__item');
   621â†’                if (listItem) {
   622â†’                    console.log('Showing corporate nav item:', linkText);
   623â†’                    listItem.style.display = '';
   624â†’                }
   625â†’            }
   626â†’        });
   627â†’        
   628â†’        // Add Session 10 to Module 03 navigation when in corporate mode
   629â†’        addSession10Navigation();

   631â†’
   632â†’    function addSession10Navigation() {
   633â†’        // Find Session 9 in Module 03 navigation and add Session 10 after it
   634â†’        const session9Link = document.querySelector('a[href*="Session9_Production_Agent_Deployment"]');
   635â†’        if (session9Link) {
   636â†’            const session9Item = session9Link.closest('.md-nav__item');
   637â†’            
   638â†’            // Check for ANY existing Session 10 navigation items - not just corporate ones
   639â†’            const existingSession10 = document.querySelector('a[href*="session10"], a[href*="Session10"], .bmw-corporate-nav-item, a[href*="Enterprise_Integration"]');
   640â†’            
   641â†’            if (session9Item && !existingSession10) {
   642â†’                console.log('ğŸ”§ Adding Session 10 to corporate navigation');
   643â†’                
   644â†’                // Create Session 10 navigation item
   645â†’                const session10Item = document.createElement('li');
   646â†’                session10Item.className = 'md-nav__item bmw-corporate-nav-item';
   647â†’                
   648â†’                const session10Link = document.createElement('a');
   649â†’                session10Link.href = '#session10-corporate-only';
   650â†’                session10Link.className = 'md-nav__link bmw-corporate-link';
   651â†’                session10Link.textContent = 'Session 10 - Enterprise Integration';
   652â†’                
   653â†’                // Add click handler to load corporate content
   654â†’                session10Link.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
   655â†’                    e.preventDefault();
   656â†’                    loadCorporateSession10();
   657â†’                });
   658â†’                
   659â†’                session10Item.appendChild(session10Link);
   660â†’                
   661â†’                // Insert after Session 9
   662â†’                session9Item.parentNode.insertBefore(session10Item, session9Item.nextSibling);
   663â†’                
   664â†’                console.log('âœ… Session 10 added to corporate navigation');
   665â†’            } else if (existingSession10) {
   666â†’                console.log('ğŸ“„ Session 10 navigation already exists, skipping creation');
   667â†’            }
   668â†’        }
   669â†’        
   670â†’        // Also update the "Next" link on Session 9 to point to Session 10
   671â†’        updateSession9NextLink();
   672â†’    }
   673â†’
   674â†’    function updateSession9NextLink() {
   675â†’        // Find "Next" navigation links and update Session 9 to point to Session 10
   676â†’        const nextLinks = document.querySelectorAll('.md-footer__link--next');
   677â†’        nextLinks.forEach(link => {
   678â†’            if (window.location.pathname.includes('Session9_Production_Agent_Deployment')) {
   679â†’                const titleDiv = link.querySelector('.md-ellipsis');
   680â†’                if (titleDiv) {
   681â†’                    titleDiv.textContent = 'Session 10 - Enterprise Integration';
   682â†’                    link.href = '#session10-corporate-only';
   683â†’                    
   684â†’                    // Add click handler for corporate Session 10
   685â†’                    link.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
   686â†’                        e.preventDefault();
   687â†’                        loadCorporateSession10();
   688â†’                    });
   689â†’                    
   690â†’                    console.log('ğŸ”§ Updated Session 9 next link to point to Session 10');
   691â†’                }
   692â†’            }
   693â†’        });
   694â†’    }
   695â†’
   696â†’    // Track if Session 10 content is currently loaded to prevent multiple loads
   697â†’    let session10Loaded = false;
   698â†’    
   699â†’    window.loadCorporateSession10 = async function() {
   700â†’        console.log('ğŸ” Loading corporate Session 10 content...');
   701â†’        
   702â†’        // Prevent multiple loads of Session 10 content
   703â†’        if (session10Loaded) {
   704â†’            console.log('ğŸ“„ Session 10 already loaded, skipping...');
   705â†’            return true;
   706â†’        }
   707â†’        
   708â†’        // Retry mechanism for improved reliability
   709â†’        const maxRetries = 3;
   710â†’        let retryCount = 0;
   711â†’        
   712â†’        while (retryCount < maxRetries) {
   713â†’            try {
   714â†’                console.log(`ğŸ”„ Attempt ${retryCount + 1}/${maxRetries} to load Session 10...`);
   715â†’                
   716â†’                // Check if corporate content loader exists
   717â†’                if (!window.CorporateContentLoader) {
   718â†’                    console.warn('âš ï¸ Corporate content loader not available, waiting...');
   719â†’                    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 500));
   720â†’                    retryCount++;
   721â†’                    continue;
   722â†’                }
   723â†’                
   724â†’                // If content is not loaded yet, try to load it first
   725â†’                if (!window.CorporateContentLoader.loadedContent) {
   726â†’                    console.log('ğŸ“¥ Corporate content not loaded yet, loading now...');
   727â†’                    const loaded = await window.CorporateContentLoader.load();
   728â†’                    if (!loaded) {
   729â†’                        console.warn('âš ï¸ Failed to load corporate content, retrying...');
   730â†’                        retryCount++;
   731â†’                        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));
   732â†’                        continue;
   733â†’                    }
   734â†’                    console.log('âœ… Corporate content loaded successfully');
   735â†’                }
   736â†’                
   737â†’                // Now check for Session 10 content
   738â†’                const session10Content = window.CorporateContentLoader.loadedContent['03_mcp-acp-a2a/Session10_Enterprise_Integration_Production_Deployment.md'];
   739â†’                if (session10Content) {
   740â†’                    console.log('ğŸ“„ Found Session 10 content, replacing page...');
   741â†’                    session10Loaded = true;
   742â†’                    
   743â†’                    // Update page title
   744â†’                    document.title = 'Session 10: Enterprise Integration & Production Deployment | Agentic AI Nano-Degree';
   745â†’                    
   746â†’                    // Update URL without causing page reload - use hash instead of path to avoid 404s
   747â†’                    if (history.pushState) {
   748â†’                        // Use hash-based navigation to avoid creating non-existent paths
   749â†’                        const baseUrl = window.location.pathname.replace(/#.*$/, '');
   750â†’                        const newUrl = baseUrl + '#session10-corporate-content';
   751â†’                        history.pushState({page: 'session10'}, '', newUrl);
   752â†’                    }
   753â†’                    
   754â†’                    // Replace page content
   755â†’                    await window.CorporateContentLoader.replacePageContent(session10Content);
   756â†’                    
   757â†’                    // Wait a bit for content to be injected, then update navigation
   758â†’                    setTimeout(async () => {
   759â†’                        await updateMkDocsNavigationForCorporateContent(session10Content);
   760â†’                    }, 100);
   761â†’                    
   762â†’                    // Instantly jump to top of the page after content is loaded
   763â†’                    setTimeout(() => {
   764â†’                        window.scrollTo(0, 0);
   765â†’                        console.log('ğŸ“ Jumped to top of Session 10 content');
   766â†’                    }, 200);
   767â†’                    
   768â†’                    console.log('âœ… Session 10 corporate content loaded successfully');
   769â†’                    return true;
   770â†’                    
   771â†’                } else {
   772â†’                    console.warn('âš ï¸ Session 10 content not found in encrypted data, retrying...');
   773â†’                    console.log('Available content keys:', Object.keys(window.CorporateContentLoader.loadedContent || {}));
   774â†’                    retryCount++;
   775â†’                    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));
   776â†’                    continue;
   777â†’                }
   778â†’                
   779â†’            } catch (error) {
   780â†’                console.warn(`âš ï¸ Error loading Session 10 (attempt ${retryCount + 1}):`, error);
   781â†’                retryCount++;
   782â†’                if (retryCount < maxRetries) {
   783â†’                    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 1000));
   784â†’                }
   785â†’            }
   786â†’        }
   787â†’        
   788â†’        console.error('âŒ Failed to load Session 10 after all retries');
   789â†’        return false;
   790â†’    }
   791â†’
   792â†’    async function updateMkDocsNavigationForCorporateContent(contentMarkdown) {
   793â†’        console.log('ğŸ”§ Updating MkDocs navigation for corporate content...');
   794â†’        
   795â†’        // No guard needed - we're already on a corporate content page if this runs
   796â†’        
   797â†’        try {
   798â†’            // Extract metadata from the content itself
   799â†’            const contentMetadata = extractContentMetadata(contentMarkdown);
   800â†’            console.log('ğŸ“„ Detected content metadata:', contentMetadata);
   801â†’            
   802â†’            // Wait for MkDocs navigation to be ready (retry mechanism)
   803â†’            let attempts = 0;
   804â†’            const maxAttempts = 5;
   805â†’            let corporateNavItem = null;
   806â†’            
   807â†’            while (!corporateNavItem && attempts < maxAttempts) {
   808â†’                if (attempts > 0) {
   809â†’                    await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, 200 * attempts)); // Progressive delay
   810â†’                }
   811â†’                
   812â†’                // Debug: List all navigation links on first attempt
   813â†’                if (attempts === 0) {
   814â†’                    const allNavLinks = document.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__link');
   815â†’                    console.log('ğŸ” Debug - All navigation links found:', allNavLinks.length);
   816â†’                    console.log('ğŸ” Navigation structure:', Array.from(allNavLinks).slice(0, 10).map(link => ({
   817â†’                        href: link.getAttribute('href'),
   818â†’                        text: link.textContent.trim(),
   819â†’                        active: link.classList.contains('md-nav__link--active')
   820â†’                    })));
   821â†’                }
   822â†’                
   823â†’                // First try to find current active navigation item
   824â†’                corporateNavItem = document.querySelector('.md-nav__link--active')?.closest('.md-nav__item');
   825â†’                
   826â†’                if (!corporateNavItem) {
   827â†’                    // Try specific Session 9 patterns
   828â†’                    const session9Selectors = [
   829â†’                        'a[href*="Session9_Production_Agent_Deployment"]',
   830â†’                        'a[href*="Session9"]',
   831â†’                        'a[href*="Production_Agent_Deployment"]'
   832â†’                    ];
   833â†’                    
   834â†’                    for (const selector of session9Selectors) {
   835â†’                        corporateNavItem = document.querySelector(selector)?.closest('.md-nav__item');
   836â†’                        if (corporateNavItem) {
   837â†’                            console.log(`ğŸ¯ Found via selector: ${selector}`);
   838â†’                            break;
   839â†’                        }
   840â†’                    }
   841â†’                }
   842â†’                
   843â†’                if (!corporateNavItem) {
   844â†’                    // Fallback: try any MCP/ACP section navigation item
   845â†’                    corporateNavItem = document.querySelector([
   846â†’                        'a[href*="03_mcp-acp-a2a"]',
   847â†’                        'a[href*="mcp-acp-a2a"]'
   848â†’                    ].join(', '))?.closest('.md-nav__item');
   849â†’                }
   850â†’                
   851â†’                attempts++;
   852â†’                console.log(`ğŸ” Navigation search attempt ${attempts}/${maxAttempts}, found:`, !!corporateNavItem);
   853â†’                
   854â†’                if (corporateNavItem) {
   855â†’                    const navLink = corporateNavItem.querySelector('.md-nav__link');
   856â†’                    console.log('ğŸ” Found navigation item:', {
   857â†’                        href: navLink?.getAttribute('href'),
   858â†’                        text: navLink?.textContent?.trim(),
   859â†’                        outerHTML: corporateNavItem.outerHTML.substring(0, 200) + '...'
   860â†’                    });
   861â†’                }
   862â†’            }
   863â†’            
   864â†’            if (corporateNavItem) {
   865â†’                // Remove active state from all navigation items
   866â†’                document.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__item').forEach(item => {
   867â†’                    item.classList.remove('md-nav__item--active');
   868â†’                    const link = item.querySelector('.md-nav__link');
   869â†’                    if (link) {
   870â†’                        link.classList.remove('md-nav__link--active');
   871â†’                    }
   872â†’                });
   873â†’                
   874â†’                // Activate corporate content navigation item
   875â†’                corporateNavItem.classList.add('md-nav__item--active');
   876â†’                const corporateLink = corporateNavItem.querySelector('.md-nav__link');
   877â†’                if (corporateLink) {
   878â†’                    corporateLink.classList.add('md-nav__link--active');
   879â†’                    // Update the link text to match current content
   880â†’                    if (contentMetadata.title) {
   881â†’                        corporateLink.textContent = contentMetadata.title;
   882â†’                    }
   883â†’                }
   884â†’                
   885â†’                // Create corporate content sub-navigation based on content structure
   886â†’                createCorporateContentSubNavigation(corporateNavItem, contentMetadata);
   887â†’                
   888â†’                // Scroll corporate content item into view in sidebar
   889â†’                corporateNavItem.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'nearest' });
   890â†’                
   891â†’                console.log(`âœ… MkDocs navigation updated for ${contentMetadata.title || 'corporate content'}`);
   892â†’            } else {
   893â†’                console.warn('âš ï¸ Corporate content navigation item not found');
   894â†’            }
   895â†’            
   896â†’            // Fix potential sidebar styling conflicts
   897â†’            fixSidebarStylingConflicts();
   898â†’            
   899â†’        } catch (error) {
   900â†’            console.error('âŒ Failed to update MkDocs navigation for corporate content:', error);
   901â†’        }
   902â†’    }
   903â†’
   904â†’    function extractContentMetadata(markdownContent) {
   905â†’        const metadata = {
   906â†’            title: null,
   907â†’            sections: [],
   908â†’            type: 'corporate-content'
   909â†’        };
   910â†’        
   911â†’        if (!markdownContent) return metadata;
   912â†’        
   913â†’        // Extract title from first H1
   914â†’        const titleMatch = markdownContent.match(/^#\s+(.+)$/m);
   915â†’        if (titleMatch) {
   916â†’            metadata.title = titleMatch[1].trim();
   917â†’        }
   918â†’        
   919â†’        // Extract sections from H2 and H3 headings
   920â†’        const headingMatches = markdownContent.match(/^#{2,3}\s+(.+)$/gm);
   921â†’        if (headingMatches) {
   922â†’            metadata.sections = headingMatches.map(heading => {
   923â†’                const level = (heading.match(/#/g) || []).length;
   924â†’                const title = heading.replace(/^#+\s+/, '').trim();
   925â†’                const id = title.toLowerCase()
   926â†’                    .replace(/[^a-z0-9\s-]/g, '')
   927â†’                    .replace(/\s+/g, '-')
   928â†’                    .replace(/-+/g, '-')
   929â†’                    .replace(/^-|-$/g, '');
   930â†’                
   931â†’                return {
   932â†’                    level,
   933â†’                    title,
   934â†’                    id: id || title.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-'),
   935â†’                    href: `#${id || title.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-')}`
   936â†’                };
   937â†’            });
   938â†’        }
   939â†’        
   940â†’        // Detect content type from title or content
   941â†’        if (metadata.title) {
   942â†’            if (metadata.title.includes('Session')) {
   943â†’                metadata.type = 'session';
   944â†’                // Extract session number if present
   945â†’                const sessionMatch = metadata.title.match(/Session\s*(\d+)/i);
   946â†’                if (sessionMatch) {
   947â†’                    metadata.sessionNumber = parseInt(sessionMatch[1]);
   948â†’                }
   949â†’            } else if (metadata.title.includes('Enterprise') || metadata.title.includes('Production')) {
   950â†’                metadata.type = 'enterprise-content';
   951â†’            }
   952â†’        }
   953â†’        
   954â†’        return metadata;
   955â†’    }
   956â†’
   957â†’
   958â†’    function createCorporateContentSubNavigation(navItem, contentMetadata) {
   959â†’        console.log(`ğŸ”§ Creating sub-navigation for ${contentMetadata.title || 'corporate content'}...`);
   960â†’        
   961â†’        // Remove any existing sub-navigation to rebuild with current content
   962â†’        const existingSubNav = navItem.querySelector('.md-nav');
   963â†’        if (existingSubNav) {
   964â†’            existingSubNav.remove();
   965â†’        }
   966â†’        
   967â†’        // Debug content metadata
   968â†’        console.log('ğŸ” Content metadata for sub-navigation:', contentMetadata);
   969â†’        console.log('ğŸ” Available sections:', contentMetadata.sections);
   970â†’        
   971â†’        // Only create sub-navigation if we have sections
   972â†’        if (contentMetadata.sections && contentMetadata.sections.length > 0) {
   973â†’            // Create sub-navigation structure
   974â†’            const subNav = document.createElement('nav');
   975â†’            subNav.className = 'md-nav md-nav--secondary';
   976â†’            subNav.setAttribute('aria-label', `${contentMetadata.title || 'Corporate Content'} Navigation`);
   977â†’            
   978â†’            const subNavList = document.createElement('ul');
   979â†’            subNavList.className = 'md-nav__list';
   980â†’            
   981â†’            // Create navigation items from content sections
   982â†’            contentMetadata.sections.forEach(section => {
   983â†’                const listItem = document.createElement('li');
   984â†’                listItem.className = 'md-nav__item';
   985â†’                
   986â†’                const link = document.createElement('a');
   987â†’                link.href = section.href;
   988â†’                link.className = 'md-nav__link';
   989â†’                link.textContent = section.title;
   990â†’                
   991â†’                // Add appropriate nesting class for H3 items
   992â†’                if (section.level === 3) {
   993â†’                    listItem.classList.add('md-nav__item--nested');
   994â†’                }
   995â†’                
   996â†’                // Add smooth scroll behavior for anchor links
   997â†’                link.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
   998â†’                    e.preventDefault();
   999â†’                    const targetId = section.id;
  1000â†’                    const targetElement = document.getElementById(targetId) || 
  1001â†’                                         document.querySelector(`h${section.level}[id="${targetId}"]`) ||
  1002â†’                                         findHeadingByText(section.title);
  1003â†’                    
  1004â†’                    if (targetElement) {
  1005â†’                        targetElement.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth' });
  1006â†’                        // Update URL hash
  1007â†’                        history.pushState(null, '', section.href);
  1008â†’                        
  1009â†’                        // Update active state in sub-navigation
  1010â†’                        subNavList.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__link').forEach(l => l.classList.remove('md-nav__link--active'));
  1011â†’                        link.classList.add('md-nav__link--active');
  1012â†’                    }
  1013â†’                });
  1014â†’                
  1015â†’                listItem.appendChild(link);
  1016â†’                subNavList.appendChild(listItem);
  1017â†’            });
  1018â†’            
  1019â†’            subNav.appendChild(subNavList);
  1020â†’            navItem.appendChild(subNav);
  1021â†’            
  1022â†’            console.log(`âœ… Sub-navigation created with ${contentMetadata.sections.length} sections`);
  1023â†’            
  1024â†’            // Set up scroll spy for corporate content - we're already on a corporate page
  1025â†’            setupCorporateContentScrollSpy(subNavList, contentMetadata.sections);
  1026â†’        }
  1027â†’        
  1028â†’        // Mark as corporate content for scroll spy detection
  1029â†’        document.body.classList.add('corporate-content-active');
  1030â†’        console.log('ğŸ”§ Marked page as corporate content');
  1031â†’        
  1032â†’        // Expand the navigation and ensure visibility
  1033â†’        navItem.classList.add('md-nav__item--nested', 'md-nav__item--active', 'corporate-nav-item');
  1034â†’        
  1035â†’        // Make sure the navigation item is visible and expanded
  1036â†’        const navInput = navItem.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
  1037â†’        if (navInput) {
  1038â†’            navInput.checked = true;
  1039â†’        }
  1040â†’        
  1041â†’        // Add explicit CSS to ensure visibility and prevent removal
  1042â†’        navItem.style.display = 'block !important';
  1043â†’        navItem.setAttribute('data-corporate-nav', 'true');
  1044â†’        const subNav = navItem.querySelector('.md-nav');
  1045â†’        if (subNav) {
  1046â†’            subNav.style.display = 'block !important';
  1047â†’            subNav.style.visibility = 'visible';
  1048â†’            subNav.setAttribute('data-corporate-subnav', 'true');
  1049â†’        }
  1050â†’        
  1051â†’        // Prevent navigation from being hidden by other scripts
  1052â†’        const observer = new MutationObserver((mutations) => {
  1053â†’            mutations.forEach((mutation) => {
  1054â†’                if (mutation.type === 'attributes' && mutation.attributeName === 'style') {
  1055â†’                    const target = mutation.target;
  1056â†’                    if (target.hasAttribute('data-corporate-nav') || target.hasAttribute('data-corporate-subnav')) {
  1057â†’                        if (target.style.display === 'none' || target.style.visibility === 'hidden') {
  1058â†’                            console.log('ğŸ”§ Preventing corporate navigation from being hidden');
  1059â†’                            target.style.display = 'block';
  1060â†’                            target.style.visibility = 'visible';
  1061â†’                        }
  1062â†’                    }
  1063â†’                }
  1064â†’            });
  1065â†’        });
  1066â†’        
  1067â†’        observer.observe(navItem, { attributes: true, subtree: true });
  1068â†’        if (subNav) {
  1069â†’            observer.observe(subNav, { attributes: true, subtree: true });
  1070â†’        }
  1071â†’        
  1072â†’        console.log('ğŸ”§ Navigation item expanded and protected from hiding');
  1073â†’    }
  1074â†’
  1075â†’    function findHeadingByText(text) {
  1076â†’        // Helper function to find headings by text content
  1077â†’        const headings = document.querySelectorAll('h1, h2, h3, h4, h5, h6');
  1078â†’        for (const heading of headings) {
  1079â†’            if (heading.textContent.trim().toLowerCase().includes(text.toLowerCase())) {
  1080â†’                return heading;
  1081â†’            }
  1082â†’        }
  1083â†’        return null;
  1084â†’    }
  1085â†’
  1086â†’    function setupCorporateContentScrollSpy(navList, sections) {
  1087â†’        console.log('ğŸ” Setting up scroll spy for corporate content navigation...');
  1088â†’        
  1089â†’        let ticking = false;
  1090â†’        let lastActiveSection = null;
  1091â†’        let scrollSpyActive = false;
  1092â†’        
  1093â†’        function updateActiveNavigation() {
  1094â†’            if (!navList || !sections) return;
  1095â†’            
  1096â†’            // Find which section is currently visible
  1097â†’            let activeSection = null;
  1098â†’            const scrollTop = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
  1099â†’            
  1100â†’            // Check each section to find the currently visible one
  1101â†’            for (let i = sections.length - 1; i >= 0; i--) {
  1102â†’                const section = sections[i];
  1103â†’                const targetElement = document.getElementById(section.id) || 
  1104â†’                                   document.querySelector(`h${section.level}[id="${section.id}"]`) ||
  1105â†’                                   findHeadingByText(section.title);
  1106â†’                
  1107â†’                if (targetElement) {
  1108â†’                    const rect = targetElement.getBoundingClientRect();
  1109â†’                    const elementTop = rect.top + scrollTop;
  1110â†’                    
  1111â†’                    // Consider element active if it's within the viewport or just passed
  1112â†’                    if (elementTop <= scrollTop + 100) {
  1113â†’                        activeSection = section;
  1114â†’                        break;
  1115â†’                    }
  1116â†’                }
  1117â†’            }
  1118â†’            
  1119â†’            // Update navigation highlighting if section changed
  1120â†’            if (activeSection && activeSection.id !== lastActiveSection) {
  1121â†’                // ONLY remove active state from corporate sub-navigation links, not main nav
  1122â†’                navList.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__link').forEach(link => {
  1123â†’                    link.classList.remove('md-nav__link--active');
  1124â†’                });
  1125â†’                
  1126â†’                // Add active state to current section's nav link
  1127â†’                const activeLink = navList.querySelector(`a[href="#${activeSection.id}"]`);
  1128â†’                if (activeLink) {
  1129â†’                    activeLink.classList.add('md-nav__link--active');
  1130â†’                    console.log(`ğŸ” Corporate active section: ${activeSection.title}`);
  1131â†’                }
  1132â†’                
  1133â†’                lastActiveSection = activeSection.id;
  1134â†’            }
  1135â†’            
  1136â†’            ticking = false;
  1137â†’        }
  1138â†’        
  1139â†’        function onScroll() {
  1140â†’            if (!ticking) {
  1141â†’                requestAnimationFrame(updateActiveNavigation);
  1142â†’                ticking = true;
  1143â†’            }
  1144â†’        }
  1145â†’        
  1146â†’        // Clean up any existing scroll listeners for corporate content
  1147â†’        if (window.corporateScrollListener) {
  1148â†’            window.removeEventListener('scroll', window.corporateScrollListener);
  1149â†’        }
  1150â†’        
  1151â†’        // Set up scroll listener for corporate content
  1152â†’        window.corporateScrollListener = onScroll;
  1153â†’        window.addEventListener('scroll', onScroll, { passive: true });
  1154â†’        console.log('âœ… Corporate scroll listener activated');
  1155â†’        
  1156â†’        // Initial check
  1157â†’        updateActiveNavigation();
  1158â†’        
  1159â†’        console.log('âœ… Corporate content scroll spy setup complete');
  1160â†’    }
  1161â†’
  1162â†’    function fixSidebarStylingConflicts() {
  1163â†’        console.log('ğŸ”§ Fixing sidebar styling conflicts...');
  1164â†’        
  1165â†’        // Ensure sidebar scrolling works properly
  1166â†’        const sidebar = document.querySelector('.md-sidebar--primary .md-sidebar__scrollwrap');
  1167â†’        if (sidebar) {
  1168â†’            sidebar.style.overflowY = 'auto';
  1169â†’            sidebar.style.height = 'calc(100vh - 2.4rem)';
  1170â†’        }
  1171â†’        
  1172â†’        // Fix potential z-index conflicts
  1173â†’        const sidebarContainer = document.querySelector('.md-sidebar--primary');
  1174â†’        if (sidebarContainer) {
  1175â†’            sidebarContainer.style.zIndex = '3';
  1176â†’        }
  1177â†’        
  1178â†’        // Ensure bottom navigation doesn't overlap
  1179â†’        const bottomNav = document.querySelector('.md-footer');
  1180â†’        if (bottomNav) {
  1181â†’            bottomNav.style.position = 'relative';
  1182â†’            bottomNav.style.zIndex = '1';
  1183â†’        }
  1184â†’        
  1185â†’        // Fix any content overflow issues
  1186â†’        const contentArea = document.querySelector('.md-content');
  1187â†’        if (contentArea) {
  1188â†’            contentArea.style.overflow = 'visible';
  1189â†’        }
  1190â†’        
  1191â†’        console.log('âœ… Sidebar styling conflicts fixed');
  1192â†’    }
  1193â†’
  1194â†’    function hidePublicNavigationItems() {
  1195â†’        const navigationItems = document.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__link');
  1196â†’        navigationItems.forEach(link => {
  1197â†’            const linkText = link.textContent.trim();
  1198â†’            // Hide items that contain public/local content indicators (but NOT main nav items)
  1199â†’            if (linkText.includes('Public LLM API Configuration') || 
  1200â†’                linkText.includes('Local Development Environment Setup') ||
  1201â†’                linkText.includes('Local Setup Requirements') ||
  1202â†’                linkText.includes('Setup Steps') ||
  1203â†’                linkText.includes('OpenAI Setup') ||
  1204â†’                linkText.includes('Anthropic Claude Setup') ||
  1205â†’                linkText.includes('Testing Your Setup') ||
  1206â†’                linkText.includes('Local LLM Options')) {
  1207â†’                const listItem = link.closest('.md-nav__item');
  1208â†’                if (listItem) {
  1209â†’                    console.log('Hiding public nav item:', linkText);
  1210â†’                    listItem.style.display = 'none';
  1211â†’                }
  1212â†’            }
  1213â†’        });
  1214â†’    }

  1216â†’    function removeSession10Navigation() {
  1217â†’        // Remove ALL Session 10 navigation items when in public mode
  1218â†’        const session10Selectors = [
  1219â†’            'a[href*="Session10_Enterprise_Integration"]',
  1220â†’            'a[href*="session10-corporate"]',
  1221â†’            'a[href*="Enterprise_Integration"]',
  1222â†’            '.bmw-corporate-nav-item',
  1223â†’            'a[href*="session10"]',
  1224â†’            'a[href*="Session10"]'
  1225â†’        ];
  1226â†’        
  1227â†’        session10Selectors.forEach(selector => {
  1228â†’            const session10Links = document.querySelectorAll(selector);
  1229â†’            session10Links.forEach(element => {
  1230â†’                const listItem = element.closest('.md-nav__item');
  1231â†’                if (listItem) {
  1232â†’                    console.log('ğŸ—‘ï¸ Removing Session 10 navigation item:', element.textContent?.trim() || selector);
  1233â†’                    listItem.remove();
  1234â†’                }
  1235â†’            });
  1236â†’        });
  1237â†’        
  1238â†’        // Reset Session 10 loaded flag when switching to public mode
  1239â†’        session10Loaded = false;
  1240â†’        
  1241â†’        // Update Session 9 next link to not point to Session 10
  1242â†’        const nextLinks = document.querySelectorAll('.md-footer__link--next');
  1243â†’        nextLinks.forEach(link => {
  1244â†’            if (window.location.pathname.includes('Session9_Production_Agent_Deployment')) {
  1245â†’                // Remove the next link entirely for Session 9 in public mode
  1246â†’                const titleDiv = link.querySelector('.md-ellipsis');
  1247â†’                if (titleDiv && titleDiv.textContent.includes('Session 10')) {
  1248â†’                    console.log('ğŸ—‘ï¸ Removing Session 9 next link to Session 10 in public mode');
  1249â†’                    link.style.display = 'none';
  1250â†’                }
  1251â†’            }
  1252â†’        });
  1253â†’    }
  1254â†’
  1255â†’    function showPublicNavigationItems() {
  1256â†’        const navigationItems = document.querySelectorAll('.md-nav__link');
  1257â†’        navigationItems.forEach(link => {
  1258â†’            const linkText = link.textContent.trim();
  1259â†’            // Show items that contain public/local content indicators (but NOT main nav items)
  1260â†’            if (linkText.includes('Public LLM API Configuration') || 
  1261â†’                linkText.includes('Local Development Environment Setup') ||
  1262â†’                linkText.includes('Local Setup Requirements') ||
  1263â†’                linkText.includes('Setup Steps') ||
  1264â†’                linkText.includes('OpenAI Setup') ||
  1265â†’                linkText.includes('Anthropic Claude Setup') ||

     9â†’    'use strict';
    10â†’
    11â†’    // Corporate content loader class
    12â†’    // Cache buster: 2025-09-21T14:12:00Z - Fixed coder-workspaces.png 404 error
    13â†’    class CorporateContentLoader {
    14â†’        constructor() {
    15â†’            // Use assets directory path to bypass GitHub Pages filtering
    16â†’            this.encryptedContentPath = '/agentic-ai-nano/assets/data/corporate-content.js';

    19â†’            console.log('ğŸ” Current hostname:', window.location.hostname);
    20â†’            this.corporateKey = 'bmw-corporate-network-2024-secure'; // Same as encryption script
    21â†’            this.loadedContent = null;
    22â†’            this._isReplacingContent = false; // Flag to prevent duplicate content replacement
    23â†’        }
    24â†’
    25â†’        /**
    26â†’         * Derives the same key used for encryption
    27â†’         */
    28â†’        async deriveKey(passphrase) {
    29â†’            const encoder = new TextEncoder();
    30â†’            const data = encoder.encode(passphrase);
    31â†’            const hashBuffer = await crypto.subtle.digest('SHA-256', data);
    32â†’            return await crypto.subtle.importKey(
    33â†’                'raw',
    34â†’                hashBuffer,
    35â†’                { name: 'AES-GCM' },
    36â†’                false,
    37â†’                ['decrypt']
    38â†’            );
    39â†’        }
    40â†’
    41â†’        /**
    42â†’         * Decrypts content using AES-GCM
    43â†’         */
    44â†’        async decryptContent(encryptedData, key) {
    45â†’            try {
    46â†’                const iv = this.base64ToArrayBuffer(encryptedData.iv);
    47â†’                const authTag = this.base64ToArrayBuffer(encryptedData.authTag);
    48â†’                const encrypted = this.base64ToArrayBuffer(encryptedData.encrypted);
    49â†’                
    50â†’                // Combine encrypted data with auth tag for AES-GCM
    51â†’                const ciphertext = new Uint8Array(encrypted.byteLength + authTag.byteLength);
    52â†’                ciphertext.set(new Uint8Array(encrypted), 0);
    53â†’                ciphertext.set(new Uint8Array(authTag), encrypted.byteLength);
    54â†’
    55â†’                const decrypted = await crypto.subtle.decrypt(
    56â†’                    {
    57â†’                        name: 'AES-GCM',
    58â†’                        iv: iv,
    59â†’                        tagLength: 128
    60â†’                    },
    61â†’                    key,
    62â†’                    ciphertext
    63â†’                );
    64â†’
    65â†’                return new TextDecoder().decode(decrypted);
    66â†’            } catch (error) {
    67â†’                console.error('Decryption failed:', error);
    68â†’                throw new Error('Failed to decrypt corporate content');
    69â†’            }
    70â†’        }
    71â†’
    72â†’        /**
    73â†’         * Converts base64 string to ArrayBuffer
    74â†’         */
    75â†’        base64ToArrayBuffer(base64) {
    76â†’            const binaryString = atob(base64);
    77â†’            const bytes = new Uint8Array(binaryString.length);
    78â†’            for (let i = 0; i < binaryString.length; i++) {
    79â†’                bytes[i] = binaryString.charCodeAt(i);
    80â†’            }
    81â†’            return bytes.buffer;
    82â†’        }
